| **AudioSys** | Singleton object; all sounds are methods; init on first keypress (autoplay policy). v1.1 adds `pickup()` and `deliver(count)` (pitch climbs with delivery combo). v1.9 (F8): a **gain-routing graph** — `init()` builds `master`/`sfx`/`music` gain nodes and **every voice connects to the `sfx` bus** (→ master → destination); `vol {master,sfx,music}` + `setVol(cat,v)` drive the Options sliders; `music` is the bus **`MusicSys` feeds into** as of v3.4 P6 (§2.8) — the Music slider now governs real audio; `ui(up)` is the menu blip; v2.0 (F9): `achievement()` is the unlock fanfare (a rising triad); v3.1 (P3): **`hunterborn()`** is the garbage-coalescence warning cue (two low descending sawtooth voices a dissonant tritone apart, ~0.4 s — §2.5.1/§2.8); v3.3 (P3): **`scooploss()`** is the short deflating downward blip when a scoop level is lost to damage (§2.12/§2.14.1); v3.4 (P5): **`lowhp(on)`** is the low-health voice — same persistent start/stop shape as `thrust`/`saucer`, edge-detected off one latch in `update()` and torn down at every site `thrust(false)`/`saucer(false)` already are (§2.8/§2.12); **v3.5 (P3) rebuilt it** as a pulsed root+harmonic voice (an amplitude-LFO "pulse" gain over two static-level oscillators) with a new **`lowhpSet(t)`** ramping pulse rate/gain from HP urgency, called every frame the state is engaged from the same `update()` site | Continuous sounds (thrust, saucer, **lowhp**) are start/stop node pairs. **Add new SFX connecting to `this.sfx`, not `this.ctx.destination`** (so master/SFX volume applies); follow the `now()` + gain-envelope pattern. `vol` values persist even before `ctx` exists (loadSettings sets them; init applies them). |
| **MusicSys** (v3.4 P6, layers/tracks v3.4 P7; track set replaced + intensity FROZEN v3.5) | A module **alongside** `AudioSys` (not inside it): `duck`/`trackGain` gain nodes + `layerGates` (`[{node, tier, target}]` parallel to `this.track.layers`), `setState(s)`/`setDuck(on)`/`setIntensity(f)`/`update()`, plus `ensureGraph`/`scheduleStep`/`playNote`. A **lookahead scheduler** (`update()`, called once per frame from the main loop's `updateMusic()`): each frame schedules any note starting within `MUSIC_LOOKAHEAD` (0.2 s), consuming a generic step-sequencer **track table** (`{stepDur, steps, layers:[{...}]}`) — never `setTimeout`. `setState` crossfades tracks off `game.state` via `musicStateFor()` (title→Beacon title track, playing→`MUSIC_TRACKS[settings.musicTrack]`, else→silence), and builds one persistent gate `GainNode` per layer at `(layer.tier || 1)`'s target for the current intensity. **v3.5 THE FREEZE:** no shipping track carries a `tier` field, so every gate is built at tier 1 (always on) and `setIntensity(f)` — which opens `if (lg.tier === 1) continue;` — walks the gate list and does nothing. It's still called from `nextWave()`; the v3.4-P7 machinery (`MUSIC_LAYER_THRESHOLD`, `MUSIC_LAYER_CROSSFADE`, the gate ramps) is intact but **dormant** — re-arm by adding `tier` fields back to track data, nothing else. `setDuck(menuActive())` ramps `duck` to 0.5 while a menu is open. All output routes into `AudioSys.music` (§2.8). | **Every entry point is ctx-guarded** (`if (!AudioSys.ctx) return;`) exactly like an `AudioSys` voice, so nothing starts before the first user gesture; the `duck` node is built lazily by `ensureGraph`. **Add new tracks as DATA tables in `MUSIC_TRACKS`, not code — do not touch the scheduler.** The five shipping tracks are ported **verbatim** from `tools/music-lab.html` — re-tune there, not here. `setDuck`/`setIntensity` are idempotent. **`scheduleStep` never consults intensity** — every layer is always scheduled; gating lives entirely in the downstream `layerGates` node (frozen on in v3.5), so a track's note timing/pitch is provably fixed. Tracks are WebAudio-synthesized only (no audio files — house standard). |
| **Input** | `keys{}` map + the data-driven **`bindings`** table (v1.8) + the `GP` button/axis enum + `GP_NAME` (display labels) + `REBINDABLE`/`DEFAULT_BINDINGS` (v1.9) + `gamepad` snapshot + `pollGamepad`/`handleGamepadMenu` + resolution helpers (`kbActive`/`gpActive`/`actionHeld`/`gpPressed`) + menu-nav helpers (`menuNavEdges`/`resetMenuNav`/`firstPressedButton`, v1.9) + the `input` predicate object | v1.8 (F7): `input.*()` resolves keyboard **or** first gamepad via `actionHeld(name)` → the `bindings` entry (keyboard `keys` / gamepad `buttons` / analog `axis` past `GP_DEADZONE`). **Add or rebind by editing `bindings`, never by reading `keys`/gamepad inline.** v1.9 (F8): the `keydown` handler and `handleGamepadMenu` each check **three contexts in priority order — rebind-capture, menu-open, normal-play** — so menu/capture input can't leak into `keys{}` or the ship (see §2.16). `DEFAULT_BINDINGS` is a pristine snapshot (before loadSettings) for Return-to-Defaults; `REBINDABLE` = the `fixed:false` actions. Menu/system reads (Start/A/B) remain **edge-triggered** via `gpPressed`; directional menu nav is edge-detected via the `menuNav` latch. **v3.5 (P1): the menu-open branch of the `keydown` handler now returns early on `e.repeat`** (still calling `preventDefault()`), so browser key auto-repeat can no longer fire `handleMenuKey` dozens of times per held press — matching `handleGamepadMenu`'s pre-existing edge-detected nav via `menuNavEdges()`. The rebind-capture and normal-play branches are untouched (gameplay legitimately reads held keys via `keys{}`); the volume-slider and Difficulty-toggle rows are downstream of the same branch, so held-key scrubbing on those is also gone (§2.16). |
| **Helpers** | `rand`, `randSign`, **`difficultyFactor`/`ramp`** (v1.5), **`leverScale`** (v3.4 P2), `wrap`, `dist2`, `angleTo`, **`shortDelta`** (v1.1), **`wrapOffset`/`wrapPos`** (v1.2), `glowStroke`, `drawPoly`, `COLOR` | ⚠️ `wrap`, `dist2`, `angleTo`, `shortDelta` are **wrap-aware** and now operate against `WORLD_W/WORLD_H`. Always use these for distance/aiming/link math — naive `Math.hypot` deltas break near edges. `wrapOffset` gives the nearest wrapped image of a point relative to the camera (rendering); `wrapPos` folds a fresh spawn into `[0,WORLD)`. **`difficultyFactor(wave)`** = `1−e^(−(wave−1)/RAMP_WAVES)` (0→1 ramp); **`ramp(floor, ceil, wave)`** interpolates any threat parameter through it — use these for any new wave-scaled value (§2.13). **`leverScale(lever, wave)`** (v3.4 P2) wraps `ramp` for a **difficulty lever** `{enabled, start, floor}` — pinned at `start` when disabled, else ramps `start`→`floor` (clamped, never below `floor`); see §2.13 and `DIFFICULTY-LEVERS.md`. |
| **Entity classes** | `Ship`, `Bullet`, `DebrisSatellite`, `HunterSatellite`, `Saucer`, `Particle`, and (v1.1) `Garbage`, `FloatText`, `Dock`, (v1.7) `Powerup` + `drawCanister()`/`drawPowerupGlyph()` shared renderers | Uniform contract: constructor, `update(dt)`, `draw()`, `dead` flag. v1.4: `Asteroid` → **`DebrisSatellite`** (broken-satellite silhouette; splits handled in `destroyDebris`, not a `split()` method). **v3.3 P2:** the old procedural `hull` polygon + `shards` open polylines are gone — a `DebrisSatellite` now carries **`this.art`**, a per-instance baked copy (scaled to `radius`, small random per-vertex jitter, done once in the constructor) of one `SAT_ART` archetype's polylines, and `draw()` iterates `this.art` rotated by the existing random `angle`/`spin` (§2.4). `Garbage` gained a **`mass`** field (default 1.0); `Garbage.fromNode(n)` carries `n.mass` back when a severed node becomes free garbage; `drawCanister()` takes an optional tint so low-mass scrap renders paler (v1.6). v3.1 P3 added coalescence fields (`coalesceDelay`, `pieces`); **v3.2 P1** makes `mass` **sum** on merge and `radius` **derive** as `7·√pieces`, `draw()` render a **cluster** of `pieces` mini-canisters, and a `pieces > 1` clump un-hookable — reversing FORK-2. **v3.2 P2** adds no new entity fields — a clump is destroyed via the flow function `shatterClump(g)` (below). v3.2 P3 removed `Garbage.decay` and added a `HunterSatellite.bornOfScrap` flag. **v3.3 P4 reverses both of those:** `Garbage` carries a **`decay` field again** (`GARBAGE_DECAY`, set in the ctor, counted down in `update()` **only while `pieces === 1`**, drawn with a `GARBAGE_FADE` blink; `Garbage.fromNode` inherits it via the ctor — `mass` stays the 5th ctor arg), and **`HunterSatellite.bornOfScrap` is DELETED** (FORK-5 — every Hunter drops garbage; `game.stats.hunterCoalesced` never read it, so Waste Not is unaffected). A `pieces > 1` clump is now **scoopable** in the pickup pass (9c — §2.5.1), no longer un-hookable. v1.3: `Ship` has an `hp` field; every hazard (`DebrisSatellite`/`HunterSatellite`/`Saucer`) carries a `damage` field (contact damage — see §2.12). v1.5 (F10): `Saucer` gained a **`rollFireTimer(range)`** method (wave-scaled reload/first-shot via the fire multiplier) and its aimed-fire error is now wave-scaled; shape/movement unchanged (§2.6, §2.13). v1.6 (F4): the killer `Satellite` + homing `Wedge` classes were **merged into `HunterSatellite`** — one diamond family, tiers 3/2/1, `homing` flag (large passive drift / medium+small active homing), speeds & turn rates wave-scaled at construction; splits/garbage handled in `destroyHunter`, and a `static spawnCore()` places a fresh large core off a viewport edge (§2.5). v1.7 (F6): a new **`Powerup`** class (`type` ∈ rapid/triple/health/magnet/engine) with a rotating-hexagon housing + a per-type glyph via **`drawPowerupGlyph()`** (reused by the HUD); Health is instant, the rest are timed (§2.14). **v3.4 (P2):** `Powerup.radius` and `Dock.radius` are now each `BASE_RADIUS * leverScale(LEVER, game.wave)`, baked once at construction (a fresh `Dock` every wave, so it only re-sizes at wave boundaries); the powerup pickup gate reads `p.radius` (not the `POWERUP_RADIUS` constant) so collision can't drift from the rendered size, and every other `Dock`-radius read (vane geometry, label offset, offload/combo-reset gates) routes through `dock.radius` (§2.10/§2.14). v3.3 (P1): `Garbage` gained a cached `hull` field (an array of `[x,y]` points from `makeClumpHull(radius)`) — generated once in the constructor and regenerated only at merge time in `coalesceGarbage`, never per frame; `draw()` branched hard on `pieces` (single canister vs. the cached hull polygon) instead of the old mini-canister cluster loop (§2.5.1). **v3.5 (P2) reverses this:** `this.hull` and `makeClumpHull` are DELETED entirely (constructor, `coalesceGarbage`'s merge, and the partial-scoop leftover re-derivation in the pickup pass all just drop the field). `drawCanister(x, y, angle, alpha, color, scale = 1)` gains a trailing `scale` param (the two pre-existing call sites — the single canister and the chain-node render loop — omit it and stay byte-identical); `Garbage.draw()`'s `pieces > 1` branch now calls it once at `scale = this.radius / 7` instead of drawing the cached hull (§2.5.1). **v3.6 (P1a): the `pieces > 1` branch's colour lerp is gone** — it now picks `COLOR.garbageLight`/`COLOR.garbage` off `this.mass / this.pieces`, the same rule the `pieces === 1` branch already used (§2.5.1). |
| **game object** | Central state: entity arrays, score/wave, spawn timers. The passive hazard array is **`game.debris`** (was `game.asteroids`, v1.4); the active-homer array is **`game.hunters`** (v1.6 — merged `game.satellites` + `game.wedges` into one), fed by **`game.hunterTimer`** (was `satelliteTimer`) and, as of v3.1 P3, **also by `coalesceGarbage`** — a coalesced Hunter is pushed straight to `game.hunters` **independent of `hunterTimer`**, so concurrent lineages are possible (§2.5.1). v1.1 adds `garbage`, `chain`, `floaters`, `dock`, `deliveryCount`, `offloadTimer`; v3.1 P3: each `game.garbage` canister carries **`coalesceDelay`** (v3.3 P4: a **3 s** activation countdown) and **`pieces`** (fused-clump count); v3.2 P1: `pieces > 1` also drives a summed **`mass`**, a derived **`radius`**, and a cluster render; **v3.3 P4: a single carries a `decay` clock again (`GARBAGE_DECAY`, singles only) and a `pieces > 1` clump is now scoopable, not un-hookable; the coalesced-Hunter `bornOfScrap` flag is gone** (§2.5.1). The per-game `game.stats` bag swapped `garbageDecayed` for **`hunterCoalesced`** (Waste Not, §2.17). v3.0 P6 (B-8) adds **`cargoMax`** (runtime tow cap, `CARGO_BASE`→`CARGO_CAP_MAX`, reset in `startGame`, grown at the dock-offload site). v1.2 adds **`camera` `{x,y}`**. v1.3 removes `lives`/`nextExtraLife`/`respawnTimer` and adds **`nextRepair`**; HP lives on `game.ship.hp`. v1.7 (F6) adds **`powerups`**, **`powerFx`** `{rapid,triple,magnet,engine}`, and **`healthTimer`**; v3.0 P5 adds **`powerBudget`** `{rapid,triple,magnet}` (count-mode shots/pieces remaining, parallel to `powerFx`; the persisted `settings` `{shotPowerupMode,magnetMode}` object is module-level, not on `game`). **v3.3 P3 adds `scoopLevel` (0–5) and `scoopHits`** (the persistent Scoop upgrade + its damage tally, reset in `startGame`, NOT in `powerFx`/`powerBudget` — §2.14.1). v1.9 (F8) adds **`game.menu`** `{screen, index, row, col, rebinding}` (v3.0 P4 also `achReturn`) — the pause-menu cursor/capture state; `game.paused` is true iff a menu screen is open (v3.0 P4: **in any state**, not only `playing`). v2.0 (F9) adds **`game.stats`** (a flat per-game achievement-counter bag, built by `resetGameStats()`) and **`game.toasts`** (active unlock banners). **v3.6 P5 adds `deathT` (seconds left in the `dying` spectacle) and `shake` (current screen-shake amplitude, px)** — both reset in `startGame`, armed in `killShip`, decayed/counted-down in `updateDeath` (§2.7/§2.9). | Single mutable global. **`game.chain` is NOT a class-entity array** — it holds plain verlet nodes (see 3.4), which now include a `mass` field. `game.camera` is set to the ship's position each frame in `update()`. **`game.paused` and `game.menu.screen` are toggled only by `openPause`/`closePause`/`quitToTitle`** (keep them in sync — `menuActive()` reads `paused`). `startGame` resets `game.menu`. |
| **Flow functions** | `startGame`, `nextWave` (also places the Dock; spawns `min(3+wave, 9)` debris — v1.4), `addScore`, `boom`, **`destroyDebris`** (v1.4; 3-way split + 3-canister emit per tier — was `destroyAsteroid`), **`destroyHunter`** (v1.6; parallel to `destroyDebris`), **`destroySaucer`** (v3.6 P3; parallel to `destroyDebris`/`destroyHunter` — the choke point for both saucer-kill sites, always drops a powerup on the saucer's own vector), **`shatterClump`** (v3.2 P2; parallel to `destroyDebris`/`destroyHunter` — destroys a `pieces > 1` clump and emits `pieces` fresh mass-split singles), **`damageShip`** (v1.3), `killShip`, `shieldDeflect`, and the v1.7 powerup helpers **`maxBullets`** (the flexible cap), **`dropPowerup`** (v3.6 P3, was `maybeDropPowerup` — an unconditional weighted-type roll, no chance gate; called by `destroySaucer`, `destroyHunter`'s large-core branch, and the dock-offload hub emission), **`spawnHealthPowerup`**, **`applyPowerup`**, plus the v3.0 P5 mode helpers **`powerMode`** (which expiry mode governs a type) and **`powerActive`** (is an effect live, honouring its mode — the one predicate the fire block/`maxBullets`/`chainMass`/Magnet/HUD all read), plus the v3.3 P3 **`inScoopBox(g)`** (the oriented-mouth capture test OR'd into the pickup pass — §2.10/§2.14.1; `applyPowerup` also gained a persistent `"scoop"` branch that raises `game.scoopLevel` outside `powerFx`/`powerBudget`, and `damageShip` erodes it). **v3.3 P4: the pickup pass itself gained a clump branch** — a `pieces > 1` clump in the capture region is scooped (lossy, mass-split into `take = min(room, pieces)` nodes; leftover re-derived + kicked by `SCOOP_SPILL_KICK`), and a single now decays via `GARBAGE_DECAY` in `Garbage.update()` (§2.5.1/§2.10). **v3.4 P4: a new **`powerDuration(type)`** helper (mirrors `powerMode`) returns the Magnet's 30 s and 15 s for everything else — read by `applyPowerup` (sets `powerFx`) and the HUD bar denominator; the Magnet pull in the pickup pass lost its `pieces === 1` gate (pulls clumps too, √mass-scaled) and reaches `MAGNET_RANGE` (380 px) with a quadratic falloff, and a clump scoop under a pieces-mode Magnet now spends `take` budget (§2.14)** | `addScore` handles the HP-repair milestone — always score through it. `destroyDebris(a, awardScore=true)` kills one debris, emits exactly `DEBRIS_GARBAGE` canisters, and pushes 3 children if `size > 1`. `destroyHunter(h, awardScore=true)` kills one Hunter: scores/booms, emits the tier's garbage (`HUNTER_GARBAGE[h.size]` normal-mass canisters at large/medium, `HUNTER_GARBAGE[1]` low-mass at small — a per-tier table as of v3.4 P1, was a flat 3 + a separate `HUNTER_SMALL_GARBAGE` = 6) for **every** Hunter of every origin (v3.3 P4 9b — the `bornOfScrap` suppression is deleted), and pushes 3 homing children if `size > 1`; called both when shot and when a homer dies on the shield. **v3.6 P5: its score AND its achievement counters (`hunterLineageKills`/`largeHunterKills`/lifetime `hunterKills`) are now BOTH gated on `awardScore` (mirroring `destroyDebris`), so the `dying`-state chain detonations — the only `awardScore=false` caller — move neither; both gameplay callers pass `true`, so live play is unchanged (before this, `awardScore=false` would have leaked lifetime `hunterKills`).** `shatterClump(g)` kills one `pieces > 1` clump: no score, boom, then exactly `g.pieces` new `Garbage` at `(g.x,g.y)` each at `mass = g.mass/g.pieces`, `pieces = 1`, a full re-armed `coalesceDelay`, and an outward `GARBAGE_SHATTER_KICK` kick — called from a new player-bullet-vs-garbage collision branch (§2.5.1/§2.10) that only targets `pieces > 1`. `damageShip(...)` is the single entry point for unshielded hits (→ `killShip` at 0 HP); self-guards on shield/hit-stun/dead. `killShip` is a respawn-free game over (still calls `scatterChain`; v2.0 also flags `game.stats.gameEnded` + runs a final `Achievements.evaluate`/`save`). **v3.6 P5: `killShip` now enters the `dying` state (arming `deathT`/`shake`) instead of jumping straight to `gameover` — but the `scatterChain`/audio teardowns and the entire achievement flush are unchanged and still fire at `killShip`; a new `updateDeath(dt)` runs the 2.5 s spectacle and flips to `gameover` at `deathT ≤ 0` (§2.7/§2.9), and `drawShockwave()` renders its expanding ring.** v2.0 (F9): `resetGameStats()` (builds the per-game `game.stats` bag) sits with the game object; the achievement **stat hooks** are one-liners inside `destroyDebris`/`destroyHunter`/`applyPowerup`/`damageShip`/`shieldDeflect`/`nextWave` (observe-at-the-source, no new indirection — §2.17). |
| **Menu / Options / Rebinding** (v1.9, F8) | `openPause`/`closePause`/`quitToTitle`/`gotoScreen`, `menuActive`, `handleMenuKey`, the `menuInput(action)` dispatcher + `menuRoot`/`menuOptions`/`menuControls`, `startRebind`/`captureKeyRebind`/`capturePadRebind`, `returnToDefaults`, and persistence (`storageOK`/`saveSettings`/`loadSettings`, `loadSettings()` called once at load) — a section after Input. v3.0 P4: `MENU_ROOT_PLAY`/`MENU_ROOT_SYS` + **`rootItems()`** (the context-aware root, replacing the single `MENU_ROOT`) | The first nested menu/UI state machine (§2.16). | **Achievements** (v2.0, F9; tiered v3.0 P7; +new v3.0 P8) | The `Achievements` module: the WEEKLY (16) + LIFETIME (19) pools, `byId`, the persisted `lifetime` counters + `weeklyUnlocked`/`lifetimeUnlocked` sets + **`lifetimeTiers{id:idx}`**, `isoWeekYear`/`poolIndex`/`selectWeekly`/`weekKeyFor`, `evaluate`/**`deriveLifetime`**/`onUnlock`/**`tierIndex`/`tierStatusText`**/`tick`/`loadCounters`, and `save`/`init` (its own **`afd_achievements_v2`** key, migrating raw counters from `_v1`) — a section after the powerup flow functions. `resetGameStats` + `powerTypesUsed` sit alongside; `TIER_NAMES`/`TIER_COLOR[]` with `COLOR`; `fmtCommas` near `drawText` | **Observes, never drives** (§2.17) — `cur()` never mutates. Stat hooks live at each event's existing site (kills/deliveries/hits/deflects/powerups/wave-clear/game-over), NOT in the module. **Tiered lifetime entries** (14 of 19) carry `tiers:[bronze..diamond]`; `evaluate()` unlocks every newly-crossed tier in one pass (ascending toasts) and persists the highest tier idx per id; the four MAX counters (`maxWave`, `maxWaveNoPowerup`, `bestDeliveredGame`, `bestDebrisGame`) update via `Math.max` at their event, the rest are sums. P8 event counters latch per-EVENT (Freight Baron on the fixed 12-in-a-visit, Zen Master on `pacifistStreak === 5`) or once-per-game at `killShip` (Daredevil, Wave Rider). `evaluate()` is called each frame from `update()` + once at game over; `deriveLifetime()` silently seeds tiers from loaded counters (no toast storm on migration). Weekly rotation deterministic (`(isoYear*52+isoWeek) % 16`, 5-wide wrapping slice); weekly unlocks reset on a new ISO week, lifetime retained. All `localStorage` access `typeof`-guarded + try/caught (never crashes). |
| **Chain physics** (v1.1) | `chainAnchor`, **`chainMass()`** (v1.4 — Σ node.mass), `wrapNode`, `updateChain`, `breakChain(i)`, `scatterChain`, `drawLink`, `drawChain` — located directly after `shieldDeflect` | See 3.4 for the physics contract. `chainMass()` drives the thrust/top-speed/tug penalties (mass sum, not count) and, v1.7, applies the Engine powerup's `ENGINE_MASS_MULT` (0.5) so all three penalties lighten from one place. `breakChain(i)` destroys node i and converts nodes i+1..end to free garbage — never splice the chain array directly. v3.0 P6 (B-8): `updateChain` relaxes over **`CHAIN_ITER` (4, was a literal 3)** passes for stability at the higher `CARGO_CAP_MAX` (**24** as of v3.4 P1, was 20) node count; the mass-penalty coefficients feeding `chainMass()`'s consumers were softened (§2.10/§2.10.2); v3.4 P1 re-validated the same stability envelope at 24 nodes without bumping `CHAIN_ITER` further (§3.4). |
| **update(dt)** | ship update → **camera-follow** → entity updates → **pickup/chain/dock pass** (v1.7: Magnet pulls free garbage here) → **`coalesceGarbage(dt)`** (v3.1 P3: garbage↔garbage magnetism + merge; a 12-piece clump becomes a Hunter — runs after the pickup loop, before `updateChain`; v3.2 P1: attraction/merge now mass-weighted + momentum-conserving, mass sums, radius derives; v3.3 P4: the transform just does `game.stats.hunterCoalesced++` — no `bornOfScrap` tag anymore; also the pickup pass above now **scoops** `pieces > 1` clumps, and `Garbage.update()` counts down `GARBAGE_DECAY` for singles) → **powerup pickup + `powerFx` countdown** (v1.7) → spawn timers (v1.7: ambient Health) → collision passes → cleanup filters (v1.7: `powerups`) → wave-clear check → heartbeat. v3.4 (P5): right after the camera-follow, a single edge-detected check (`game.ship.hp <= LOW_HP_THRESHOLD && !game.ship.dead`) drives `AudioSys.lowhp(true/false)` exactly once per transition, latched in `game.lowHpSiren`; **v3.5 (P3)** adds one more line at the same site — while the state is engaged, `AudioSys.lowhpSet(1 − hp/LOW_HP_THRESHOLD)` runs **every** frame (not edge-detected), scaling the voice's pulse rate/gain with urgency (§2.12) | Collision order matters (see 3.1). The old respawn-clearing step is gone (v1.3 — no respawn). `game.camera` is set to the ship's position right after `ship.update` (before spawns, so ship-relative spawns use the current position). | **draw()** | Starfield (v3.0 P1: two layers — far, wrap-aware, world-fixed at 1.0×; near, screen-space tiled parallax at 0.5×, both with per-star brightness) → title OR [**camera transform** → (**dock** → particles → **garbage** → **chain** → debris → hunters → saucers → **powerups** (v1.7) → bullets → ship → **floaters**) → **restore** → HUD (v1.7: active-powerup row under CARGO) → overlays]. **v3.6 (P1b): `drawWorldBoundary()` — the v2.1 dashed wrap-seam guide that used to run first inside the camera transform — is DELETED**, along with its call site and the four `BOUNDARY_*` constants; no replacement. v1.9 (F8): when `game.paused`, **`drawMenu()`** paints the pause-menu overlay (root/options/controls) — `drawMenu`/`menuPanel`/`drawRootMenu`/`drawOptionsMenu`/`drawControlsMenu`/`drawBindCell` + the `keyLabel`/`padLabel`/`axisLabel` formatters sit near `drawText`. v3.0 P4: `drawMenu()` now also overlays the **title** (inside the title block, before its early `return`) and **gameover** screens (drawn *after* the GAME OVER text so the system menu sits on top); `drawRootMenu` reads `rootItems()` and titles the panel "PAUSED" (play) or "MENU" (system) | Draw order = z-order: dock is the floor, floaters sit above the ship.
